PRIME Rural — UAT Test Case Master

Scope: Web CRM (Frappe v16) — User Management, Masters, Entrepreneur Profile, Product Profile, 27 Diagnostic Frameworks, Fellow Activity Logger, all Dashboards.
Sources of truth: Living BRD (brd.html), 27 client HTML mockups in from-client/, Monsoon Court design system, frappe_prime_rural repo (branch development).
Environment: https://stgprime-rural.dhwaniris.in/. Author: Samarth Paul, Dhwani RIS. Last updated: 28 May 2026.
Type: All Functional UI / UX Validation API Database Non-Func Security
Polarity: All Positive Negative Boundary
Priority: All P0 P1 P2

1. Overview & Test Case SchemePR-TC-OV

How to read this document, the ID scheme, and what each tag means. Read this first before running any case.

Intended audience: QA executor (manual or via Playwright), UAT signatories, development team verifying fixes. Each test case is self-contained — preconditions, steps, and expected results are explicit enough to run cold.

1.1 ID scheme

Every test case has an ID of the form PR-TC-<area>-<number> where <area> is one of:

Area codeMeaningExample
XCCross-cutting (entry, browser, responsive, auth, a11y, perf, error handling)PR-TC-XC-014
UMUser ManagementPR-TC-UM-007
MSMasters (Sector, Geography, Cohort, Business Basket, Framework Task Master, etc.)PR-TC-MS-022
EPEntrepreneur Profile (full lifecycle)PR-TC-EP-045
PRProduct ProfilePR-TC-PR-012
FW-<mid>Framework-specific (mid = m-financials, m-rawmat, m-machinery, etc.)PR-TC-FW-RAWMAT-008
ALFellow Activity LoggerPR-TC-AL-011
DB-EPS / DB-INF / DB-SAN / DB-MS / DB-INTDashboards (EP Status, Infra Monitor, Sankey, Milestone, Intervention)PR-TC-DB-INF-009
NTNotificationsPR-TC-NT-004
APIREST API layer (positive + negative payloads, auth, CSRF, rate-limit)PR-TC-API-031
DBDatabase layer (referential integrity, cascades, indexes)PR-TC-DB-007
SECSecurity (OWASP, role escalation, upload exploits)PR-TC-SEC-014

1.2 Tag legend

Each test case carries up to five tags. Their meanings:

TagValuesMeaning
TypeFunctional / UI-UX / Validation / API / Database / Non-Func / SecurityWhat is being tested. A single case may belong to one type only — multi-type cases are split.
PolarityPositive / Negative / BoundaryPositive = happy-path success; Negative = explicit failure / rejection path; Boundary = limits, edge values, max-min, on/off threshold.
PriorityP0 / P1 / P2P0 = release blocker (login, save, role gates, money calc); P1 = high (validation messages, UX, accuracy); P2 = nice-to-have (cosmetic, edge UI).
Role(s)SM / CTI / CTP / FA / SLC / DSG / AllSystem Manager, Core Team IT, Core Team Program, Field Associate (Fessociate), SELCO Executive, Designer. "All" = any logged-in user.
BRD linkSection ID, e.g. PR-OV-002bSource-of-truth section in brd.html that this case validates.

2. Test Environment, Data, & ToolsPR-TC-OV-ENV

Where to run, what to log in with, what data to seed, what to clean up.

2.1 Environments

EnvURLUseReset cycle
Staginghttps://stgprime-rural.dhwaniris.in/UAT, regression, Playwright E2EOn-request via dev team; do NOT bulk-delete via UI
Production(TBD, post go-live)Smoke tests only after each releaseNever reset

2.2 Test accounts (to be created in §3)

One account per role, named uat-<role>@dhwaniris.com. Roles to seed:

Login (email)RoleDisplay nameNotes
uat-sm@dhwaniris.comSystem ManagerUAT — SMFull admin; only one such account exists at a time on staging
uat-cti@dhwaniris.comCore Team ITUAT — CTIManages users, masters, milestones, notifications
uat-ctp@dhwaniris.comCore Team ProgramUAT — CTPEvaluation, scoring, Selection (final Incubated/Supported)
uat-fa@dhwaniris.comField Associate (Fessociate)UAT — FABlock-bound; default block to one with seeded entrepreneurs
uat-selco@dhwaniris.comSELCO ExecutiveUAT — SELCOSees Infra full, edits SELCO fields only
uat-designer@dhwaniris.comDesignerUAT — DSGLands on Branding Identity; upload-only on draft fields

2.3 Tooling

Manual exploratoryChrome (latest), Firefox (latest ESR), Edge (latest), Safari 17+
E2E automationPlaywright (TS, headless on CI; headed locally for debugging)
API testingPostman collection (manual) + Playwright API requests (automated). Auth via API key/secret header Authorization: token KEY:SECRET
Performance baselinesLighthouse (Chrome) for FCP / LCP; Playwright trace for network waterfall
Accessibility auditaxe-core (via @axe-core/playwright) + manual screen reader pass (NVDA on Windows, VoiceOver on macOS)
Browser dev toolsNetwork throttling at "Fast 3G" for offline-related cases; mobile emulation for tablet form factors

2.4 Test data conventions

  • Every record created during a test run is prefixed with [UAT] in its primary name field so cleanup is mechanical (e.g. [UAT] Test Entrepreneur 001).
  • Test files (photos / KYC docs) live under tests/fixtures/files/ — use only files from there, never personal photos.
  • Seed cohort: [UAT] Cohort 2026-27; sector: Food Processing; block: a block with at least one geography hierarchy fully populated.
  • Never run a UAT pass on a record with real entrepreneur data. If unsure, create a fresh [UAT]-prefixed copy first.

3. Role × Capability MatrixPR-TC-OV-ROLE

What each role should see and do — the negative tests in each module flip this matrix and assert the deny path.

Capability / Page SMCTICTPFASLCDSG
User Management (create / edit / disable user)✓✓view-only———
Masters (Sector, Geography, Cohort, Task Master, …)✓✓view-only———
EP Profile — create✓view✓✓ (own block)——
EP Profile — score (10 criteria)✓—✓———
EP Profile — set Final Selection (Incubated / Supported)✓—✓ (CTIT-only)———
EP Profile — 10Q + Rural E-Champ during profiling———✓——
Framework Prioritisation✓—✓✓——
All 27 frameworks (read)✓—✓✓ (assigned EPs)Infra onlyBranding only
All 27 frameworks (write / edit existing)✓—✓✓ (assigned EPs)Infra SELCO fields only · edit-onlyBranding draft fields only · edit-only
Frameworks — create new record✓—✓✓ (own block)— no create— no create
Frameworks — delete record✓—✓—— no delete— no delete
Fellow Activity Logger✓—✓ (view)✓——
EP Status Monitor dashboard✓✓✓———
Infra Monitor dashboard✓—✓—✓—
Milestone Tracker✓✓✓———
Intervention Dashboard✓—✓———
Sankey (Entrepreneur Dashboard)✓✓✓———
Notifications — receive✓receive-only✓✓✓✓
Notifications — configure triggers✓—————

Source: BRD §Role-Permission Matrix (PR-OV-004). Specialist roles (SLC, DSG) are edit-only inside their single assigned framework — no create, no delete, no access to any other workspace; every "—" is a hard denial enforced server-side (doctype permission), not just hidden from the sidebar. The deny paths are exercised by PR-TC-SEC-03x (Session-23 reconciliation).

4. Application Entry & RoutingPR-TC-XC-ENTRY

First contact with the application. Covers URL handling, redirects, deep links, route guards.

4.1 Base URL load

When a user types the staging URL into a fresh browser tab — what happens?

PR-TC-XC-001 Positive P0 Functional All
Base URL redirects unauthenticated user to the login page
Preconditions
  • Fresh browser (no cookies for the domain), open Incognito / Private window.
Steps
  1. Type https://stgprime-rural.dhwaniris.in/ in the address bar and press Enter.
Expected Browser is redirected to /login. The URL in the address bar changes (or a 302 is logged in the network tab). The login page renders with: PRIME Rural wordmark, email field, password field, "Continue with Google" button, "Forgot password?" link. No console errors. Page loads in < 2.5s on a 30 Mbps connection.

BRD: PR-OV-001 (System Architecture & Auth)

PR-TC-XC-002 Positive P0 Functional All
Already-authenticated user landing on base URL goes to their role's landing page
Preconditions
  • User has a valid session cookie (logged in within the session timeout window).
Steps
  1. While logged in, navigate to https://stgprime-rural.dhwaniris.in/.
Expected Role-based landing happens: SM/CTI → Dashboard workspace; CTP → EP Status Monitor; FA → Entrepreneurs list; SELCO → Infra Monitor; Designer → Marketing Tools / Branding Identity workspace. No flicker, no transient login form. URL ends in the role's actual landing path.

BRD: PR-OV-003, PR-UJ-* (per-role journeys)

PR-TC-XC-003 Negative P0 Functional All
Deep link to a protected page while logged out preserves the intent
Preconditions
  • Fresh browser. No session.
Steps
  1. Open https://stgprime-rural.dhwaniris.in/app/enterprenur-profile/EP-001 directly.
  2. Login redirect fires.
  3. Complete login as a user permitted to see that record.
Expected After successful login, user is redirected to the originally requested URL (the EP detail page), not the default landing page. URL parameter (typically redirect-to or next) is preserved through the auth flow.

BRD: PR-OV-001 (Auth)

PR-TC-XC-004 Negative P0 Functional All
Invalid / non-existent route shows a friendly 404, not a stack trace
Steps
  1. While logged in, navigate to /app/this-page-does-not-exist.
Expected A branded 404 page renders: Monsoon Court tokens, Octicon hero, "Page not found", a "Go to dashboard" CTA. Sidebar still visible. No Python traceback, no Frappe debug dump, no raw error JSON shown to the user.
PR-TC-XC-005 Negative P1 Functional All
Route to a record that does not exist (valid doctype, invalid name)
Steps
  1. Logged in, navigate to /app/enterprenur-profile/EP-DOES-NOT-EXIST-XYZ.
Expected "Document not found" message; suggested CTAs: "Back to list" and "Search". No 500. No blank page. URL is not mutated.
PR-TC-XC-006 Positive P1 Functional All
Browser Back/Forward navigation works across at least 10 hops
Steps
  1. From the dashboard, navigate through: EP list → an EP detail → its Frameworks tab → a Framework form → Save → back to EP → another EP → list → Activity Logger → Dashboard.
  2. Press Back 10 times.
  3. Then press Forward 5 times.
Expected Every back/forward action restores the prior route AND its scroll position. Sidebar active state matches the current route on every step. No state leak — filters from a prior list view do not contaminate a re-visit.
PR-TC-XC-007 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Browser tab title updates per route
Steps
  1. Visit five distinct pages: Login, Dashboard, EP list, an EP detail, a Framework form.
Expected Each page sets a unique <title> beginning with the page name and ending with " · PRIME Rural" (e.g. "Entrepreneurs · PRIME Rural"). EP detail title includes the entrepreneur name. No tab shows the generic "Frappe Desk".
PR-TC-XC-008 Negative P1 Functional All
URL with trailing slash, double slash, and uppercase is normalised
Steps
  1. Visit /APP/enterprenur-profile/ (note uppercase + trailing slash).
  2. Visit //app//enterprenur-profile (double slashes).
  3. Visit /app/enterprenur-profile? (trailing question mark).
Expected All three normalise to /app/enterprenur-profile (single canonical form). No duplicate history entries. No JS routing loop.
PR-TC-XC-009 Positive P2 Functional All
Refresh (F5) on a deep page preserves state
Steps
  1. Open EP Status Monitor, apply filters: District=East Khasi Hills, Cohort=2026-27, Sector=Food Processing.
  2. Press F5.
Expected After reload, the same filters are still selected (read from URL params), KPIs reflect those filters, and the chart redraws with the same dataset. No re-prompt to log in.
PR-TC-XC-010 Negative P0 Security All
Manually editing a record name in URL to one user is not allowed to see returns 403, not 404
Preconditions
  • Logged in as a Fessociate restricted to Block A.
  • An EP record exists in Block B.
Steps
  1. Manually type /app/enterprenur-profile/<EP-of-Block-B> into the address bar.
Expected 403 Forbidden page rendered (not 404, since the record exists — leaking existence vs non-existence to unauthorised users is itself an info leak; but a 404 here is acceptable as long as it is the same 404 returned for a non-existent record, so an attacker cannot infer which records exist). Either way: never shows the record's contents.

OWASP: A01 Broken Access Control. BRD: PR-OV-003.

5. Browser & Device CompatibilityPR-TC-XC-BR

Field teams use a mix of laptops; coordinators use desktops. Tablet support is best-effort. Mobile phone form factor is OUT of scope for the web CRM — fellows use the Flutter app on phones.

Officially supported browsers: Chrome ≥ 120, Firefox ESR ≥ 115, Edge ≥ 120, Safari ≥ 17. Internet Explorer is NOT supported (no IE 11 fallbacks). Minimum supported screen width = 1024 px (tablet landscape); designed-for 1280 px+.
PR-TC-XC-011 Positive P0 Non-Func All
App loads and login works on Chrome (latest)
Steps
  1. Open Chrome (latest stable). Visit base URL. Log in as SM. Navigate to dashboard, then EP list, then EP detail.
Expected All pages render with Monsoon Court tokens applied (Georgia font, cream background, teal primary actions). No console errors with severity ≥ Warning. No layout shift > 0.1 (CLS). Lighthouse Performance ≥ 70 on the dashboard on a 30 Mbps connection.
PR-TC-XC-012 Positive P0 Non-Func All
Same on Firefox ESR (latest)
Steps
  1. Repeat XC-011 on Firefox.
Expected Identical functional behaviour. Focus rings render at terracotta border-focus colour. Date picker uses the same shadcn-vue calendar (not the native browser one). Drop-down search-in-list (Combobox) behaves identically to Chrome.
PR-TC-XC-013 Positive P1 Non-Func All
Same on Edge (latest)
Steps
  1. Repeat XC-011 on Edge.
Expected Same as Chrome (shared Chromium engine). Specifically verify the Edge "translate this page" prompt does not appear inappropriately for English content.
PR-TC-XC-014 Positive P1 Non-Func All
Same on Safari (macOS 14+)
Steps
  1. Repeat XC-011 on Safari on a Mac.
Expected Behaves identically. Specifically check: file uploads (Safari has historically had quirks), date inputs (must use the custom shadcn-vue calendar, not the iOS-style spinner), CSS Grid layouts (sidebar + main).
PR-TC-XC-015 Negative P2 Non-Func All
Internet Explorer 11 is gracefully blocked, not silently broken
Steps
  1. Open the app in IE 11 (Windows 10 box).
Expected A static "Browser not supported — please use Chrome, Firefox, Edge, or Safari" page renders. No partial render of broken UI. No JS console flood.
PR-TC-XC-016 Negative P2 Non-Func All
Older Chrome (e.g. Chrome 100) — degraded but usable
Steps
  1. Open in Chrome 100 (or use a UA spoofer + a real engine snapshot).
Expected Core flows (login, EP list, save) still work. A banner may notify the user that the browser is outdated. No total breakage.
PR-TC-XC-017 Positive P1 Non-Func All
App works on a low-end Windows laptop (4 GB RAM, integrated graphics)
Steps
  1. On a 4-GB Windows 10 laptop, open the app in Chrome.
  2. Open EP Status Monitor with all charts rendered.
  3. Scroll, hover, interact for 5 minutes.
Expected No fan-spinning, no > 50 % CPU sustained, no > 600 MB tab memory. UI remains responsive — interactions complete in < 200 ms perceived. (This is the realistic field-coordinator hardware.)
PR-TC-XC-018 Positive P1 Non-Func All
App works under "Slow 3G" network throttle
Steps
  1. In Chrome DevTools, set network throttling to "Slow 3G" (400 kbps).
  2. Open the app, log in, navigate to dashboard.
Expected Pages render within 10 s. Skeleton loaders visible during fetch (no blank screens). No timeout errors. Subsequent navigations are faster due to caching (sub-2 s).
PR-TC-XC-019 Negative P1 Non-Func All
Network drop mid-save shows a clear error and the form data is not lost
Steps
  1. Open the EP edit form, fill 5 fields.
  2. In DevTools, set network to "Offline".
  3. Click Save.
Expected A banner (variant: danger) appears: "Save failed — please check your connection and try again." The form remains editable; the 5 entered values are still present. No silent failure (toast disappears in 3 s); the banner persists until dismissed.
PR-TC-XC-020 Positive P1 UI / UX All
App handles two simultaneous tabs of the same record without data loss
Steps
  1. Open the same EP record in Tab A and Tab B.
  2. In Tab A, edit Phone Number and save.
  3. In Tab B (without refreshing), edit Email and save.
Expected On Tab B save: a "This document was modified after you loaded it. Refresh to see the latest." dialog appears. User picks Refresh; Tab B reloads with Tab A's phone number and Tab B's email field empty again. No silent overwrite of Tab A's change.

Frappe's standard "modified mismatch" guard. Verify it actually fires.

6. Responsive Layout & Screen SizesPR-TC-XC-RP

Different laptop screens, common docking dual-monitor setups, and zoom levels. NO mobile-phone scope — fellows use the Flutter app.

BreakpointWidthLayout behaviour
xl≥ 1280 pxSidebar expanded (240 px), main content max 1280 px
lg1024–1279 pxSidebar collapsed to 64 px icon rail; labels on hover
md768–1023 pxSidebar hidden by default; hamburger top-left opens it as a drawer
sm< 768 pxSame as md — best-effort, not supported for daily field use
PR-TC-XC-021 Positive P0 UI / UX All
1920×1080 (standard desktop): sidebar expanded, main content max 1280 px centred
Steps
  1. Open the app at 1920×1080.
  2. Visit the dashboard, EP list, an EP detail, a framework form.
Expected Sidebar 240 px on the left. Main content area maxes at 1280 px and is centred (or left-aligned per spec; verify both sides have visual margins to the viewport edges if the content is left-aligned). No horizontal scrollbar at any scroll position. No element bleeds past the viewport.
PR-TC-XC-022 Positive P0 UI / UX All
1366×768 (most common low-end laptop): everything fits, no horizontal scroll
Steps
  1. Resize browser to 1366×768.
  2. Visit dashboard, then a framework form with 8+ tabs, then a child-table-heavy form.
Expected Sidebar expanded (still ≥ 1280). KPI grids reflow to 2-column on dashboards (not 4). Form fields wrap to single-column where appropriate. Tabs row scrolls horizontally with chevrons rather than wrapping. Tables show horizontal scroll within the table container only — page itself never horizontally scrolls.
PR-TC-XC-023 Positive P1 UI / UX All
1024×768 (tablet landscape / iPad / Surface): sidebar collapses to icon rail
Steps
  1. Resize to 1024×768.
Expected Sidebar is now 64 px showing icons only. Hovering an icon shows a tooltip with the label. Clicking still navigates. Page header remains visible. Filter bars on list pages collapse to a "Filters" dropdown rather than spreading wide.
PR-TC-XC-024 Positive P2 UI / UX All
800×600 (very old projector / boardroom display): no broken layout, sidebar hidden behind hamburger
Steps
  1. Resize to 800×600.
Expected Sidebar hidden by default. Hamburger button visible top-left of main content. Tapping it opens sidebar as a slide-in drawer. Closing the drawer (Escape or backdrop click) returns to the page. Charts may switch to a single-column stack.
PR-TC-XC-025 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Browser zoom 50 % to 200 % does not break layout
Steps
  1. At 1920×1080, set browser zoom to 50 %, 75 %, 100 %, 125 %, 150 %, 200 %.
  2. At each, visit dashboard, EP list, EP form.
Expected Text remains legible at all zooms. No overlapping elements. No clipped buttons. Layout reflows according to effective viewport width. (Browser zoom is the most common accessibility accommodation for low-vision users.)
PR-TC-XC-026 Negative P1 UI / UX All
No UI distortion when very long values are entered in form fields
Steps
  1. On the EP form, enter an Enterprise Name of 200 characters (within field max).
  2. Save and re-open.
Expected The field grows vertically or truncates with ellipsis; it does NOT overflow the form column. The list view shows the value with ellipsis at column width and a tooltip on hover with the full text. Cards on dashboards using the same field truncate gracefully (no horizontal scroll inside a card).
PR-TC-XC-027 Negative P1 UI / UX All
No UI distortion when a child table has 100+ rows
Steps
  1. On a Raw Materials framework form, add 100 rows to the "Required Raw Materials" child table (use API to seed).
  2. Open the form in the UI.
Expected The child table renders with internal vertical scroll, header stays sticky inside the table container. Total form scroll still smooth (no jank). Save is not blocked. Pagination or virtual scrolling kicks in if > 50 rows.
PR-TC-XC-028 Negative P1 UI / UX All
No UI distortion when a list view has 500+ records
Steps
  1. Open EP list with 500+ records (filter cleared).
  2. Scroll, hover, sort, filter.
Expected List uses server-side pagination (default 20 / page); page transitions feel instant. Filter changes refetch; sort changes refetch. No client-side full-table load.
PR-TC-XC-029 Negative P1 UI / UX All
Dropdown / Combobox with 1,000+ options stays usable
Steps
  1. Sector field — assuming > 100 sectors exist (multi-tier expansion of the master), open its dropdown.
  2. Try Village field on EP form with 1,000+ villages.
Expected Dropdown opens within 200 ms even with 1,000 options. Type-ahead filters within the dropdown debounced at 200 ms. No "freezing" of the page. Selection works on first click.
PR-TC-XC-030 Positive P2 UI / UX All
Empty-state pages render correctly when there is no data yet
Steps
  1. As a freshly-created Fessociate with no assigned EPs, open the Entrepreneurs list.
  2. Open Activity Logger with no log entries.
  3. Open a dashboard for a cohort with zero records.
Expected Each surface shows an EmptyState: 24px Octicon, "No entrepreneurs assigned yet" headline, helper text, optional primary CTA (e.g. "Add your first entrepreneur" if the user has create permission, otherwise none). NO broken charts. NO "Loading…" spinner stuck forever.

7. Login & SessionPR-TC-XC-AUTH

Web auth = email/password OR Google SSO. MSG91 / OTP is OUT of scope (removed). Session = Frappe session cookie + CSRF.

Auth scope: Mobile = Google SSO only. Web = email/password OR Google SSO. Both web flows produce the same Frappe session. There is no OTP path on the web. (BRD: PR-OV-001 Auth.)

7.1 Email / Password

PR-TC-XC-031 Positive P0 Functional All
Valid email + password logs in and lands on role landing page
Steps
  1. Open /login.
  2. Type a valid email and password for the SM role.
  3. Click Sign in.
Expected Redirected to the SM landing page in < 1.5 s. Frappe session cookie (sid) is set HttpOnly, Secure (because HTTPS), SameSite=Lax. CSRF token is captured into the page boot data. Sidebar shows the user's avatar with initials and full name.
PR-TC-XC-032 Negative P0 Functional All
Wrong password shows a clear error and does NOT reveal whether the email exists
Steps
  1. Login form: enter a valid email but wrong password.
  2. Submit.
Expected Error displays inline above the form: "Invalid email or password." — generic enough that an attacker cannot enumerate valid emails. The password field is cleared; the email field is preserved. No 500. No password ever echoed back into the field.

OWASP A07 Auth Failures (do not leak account existence).

PR-TC-XC-033 Negative P0 Functional All
Non-existent email shows the same generic error as wrong password
Steps
  1. Submit with email not-a-real-user@example.com and any password.
Expected Same generic message as XC-032: "Invalid email or password." Same response time (no timing oracle).
PR-TC-XC-034 Negative P1 Validation All
Empty email or empty password is rejected client-side before submit
Steps
  1. Leave email blank, type a password, submit.
  2. Type an email, leave password blank, submit.
Expected Inline error under the blank field: "Email is required." / "Password is required." Submit button does not fire a network request.
PR-TC-XC-035 Negative P1 Validation All
Malformed email is rejected client-side
Steps
  1. Email = not-an-email; password = anything; submit.
  2. Email = foo@; submit.
  3. Email = foo@bar (no TLD); submit.
Expected All three blocked client-side with "Enter a valid email" inline error. No network request.
PR-TC-XC-036 Negative P0 Security All
Brute-force protection: 5 consecutive failed logins locks the account or triggers a delay
Steps
  1. Repeat 6 wrong-password attempts in < 1 minute for the same email.
Expected By the 6th attempt, either: (a) account is temporarily locked with a "Too many failed attempts. Try again in N minutes." message, OR (b) a captcha appears, OR (c) exponential delay kicks in. Subsequent valid login still works after the cooldown.

OWASP A07; Frappe default lockout settings.

PR-TC-XC-037 Negative P0 Security All
Password input is type=password and masks characters by default
Steps
  1. Inspect the password input element.
Expected type="password". A "show password" toggle eye-icon exists (Octicon eye); clicking flips to type=text and back. Toggle defaults to hidden. Browser autofill is permitted (autocomplete="current-password").
PR-TC-XC-038 Positive P1 Functional All
"Forgot password" sends a reset email
Steps
  1. Click "Forgot password?" link on login.
  2. Enter a valid registered email.
  3. Submit.
Expected A confirmation banner: "If an account exists for that email, a reset link has been sent." (Worded so as not to leak existence.) The email arrives within 2 minutes, contains a one-time reset link valid for 60 minutes, link expires after first use.
PR-TC-XC-039 Negative P1 Security All
"Forgot password" for a non-existent email shows the same banner — no enumeration
Steps
  1. Submit forgot-password with an email that does not exist.
Expected Same banner as XC-038. Response time within ± 200 ms of the positive case (no timing oracle).
PR-TC-XC-040 Negative P0 Security All
Reset link cannot be used twice
Steps
  1. Use a reset link to set a new password.
  2. Try the same link again.
Expected Second use shows "This reset link has already been used or has expired" and a CTA to request a new one. No login is granted.

7.2 Google SSO

PR-TC-XC-041 Positive P0 Functional All
"Continue with Google" completes login for a pre-provisioned Google account
Steps
  1. Click "Continue with Google" on the login page.
  2. Pick the test Google account already mapped to a Frappe user.
  3. Approve scopes if prompted.
Expected OAuth round-trip completes; user lands on role landing page. Frappe session cookie set. Audit log records a Google SSO login event.
PR-TC-XC-042 Negative P0 Functional All
Google account not mapped to a Frappe user is denied with a clear message
Steps
  1. Click "Continue with Google", pick a Gmail account that has no Frappe user.
Expected Returns to login with banner: "This Google account is not authorised. Please contact your administrator." No user record auto-created. No partial session created.
PR-TC-XC-043 Negative P1 Functional All
User cancels Google consent — returns to login cleanly
Steps
  1. Click Continue with Google. At Google's consent screen, click Cancel.
Expected Returns to /login with no error banner. Fields cleared. No half-session.

7.3 Session lifecycle

PR-TC-XC-044 Positive P0 Functional All
Logout terminates the session and clears the cookie
Steps
  1. Logged in, click the user avatar → Sign out.
  2. Try Back-button to return to a protected page.
Expected Redirected to /login. Session cookie cleared. Back-button attempt to a protected page redirects again to login (not served from disk cache).
PR-TC-XC-045 Negative P1 Functional All
Session times out after configured idle period (default Frappe: ~ 8 h)
Steps
  1. Log in, leave the tab idle for the timeout duration.
  2. Try to navigate or save.
Expected Save returns 401/403 with a "Your session has expired. Please log in again." dialog. Form data not lost — re-login returns to the page with values preserved (or, at minimum, the user is told before redirect).
PR-TC-XC-046 Negative P0 Security All
Session cookie attributes are correct (HttpOnly, Secure, SameSite)
Steps
  1. After login, inspect cookies in DevTools.
Expected sid cookie has: HttpOnly = true (not accessible to JS), Secure = true (HTTPS-only), SameSite=Lax (or Strict). CSRF token cookie (if present) has the same attributes.
PR-TC-XC-047 Negative P0 Security All
CSRF protection: a state-changing request without a valid CSRF token is rejected
Steps
  1. Capture a logged-in user's session cookie.
  2. Send a POST to /api/method/frappe.client.set_value from a separate origin (or via Postman) WITHOUT the X-Frappe-CSRF-Token header.
Expected Server returns 403 with "CSRF Token Missing" or similar. The DB is not mutated.
PR-TC-XC-048 Positive P1 Functional All
Concurrent login on two devices: both sessions remain valid
Steps
  1. Log in on Device A.
  2. Log in on Device B with the same user.
  3. Action on Device A.
  4. Action on Device B.
Expected Both sessions work. (Frappe default permits concurrent sessions. If this is changed for security reasons, both clients must be told gracefully.)
PR-TC-XC-049 Negative P1 Security All
Stolen sid cookie reused from a different IP — session is invalidated within a reasonable time
Steps
  1. Log in from IP A.
  2. Replay the sid cookie from IP B (via Postman or another machine) within 30 seconds.
  3. Repeat after 1 hour.
Expected If session-IP-binding is enabled (preferred for an admin tool): the IP-B replay is rejected with 401. Without IP binding, this is informational only.
PR-TC-XC-050 Positive P2 Functional All
"Remember me" (if present) extends session lifetime correctly
Steps
  1. Log in with Remember me checked. Close browser. Reopen the next day.
Expected User is still logged in (within the extended TTL). Without Remember me, the session expires at browser close.

8. UI / UX Rules — Monsoon Court CompliancePR-TC-XC-UX

Per the Monsoon Court design system. These rules apply to every page; a violation on any one is a P1 bug because it indicates the design system is not the source of truth.

Tokens to verify visually: teal #0E4D4E, sea #1A6B6D, terracotta #C26849, cream #FBF5E5. Typeface: Georgia. No yellow, no green, no sans-serif anywhere.
PR-TC-XC-051 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Georgia is the only typeface on every page
Steps
  1. On the dashboard, EP list, EP detail, a framework form, the activity logger — inspect computed font-family for body, headers, buttons, table cells, badges, tabs, KPI values.
Expected Every text element computes font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif. No element ever resolves to sans-serif, Arial, Helvetica, Inter, system-ui, or any other family.
PR-TC-XC-052 Positive P1 UI / UX All
No green and no yellow appear anywhere in the UI
Steps
  1. Visually scan every page for green / yellow elements.
  2. Search the rendered CSS for any colour matching green, yellow, #2ecc71, #f1c40f, similar hexes.
Expected Zero green elements. Success states use teal #0E4D4E. Zero yellow elements. Warning states use terracotta #C26849.

Monsoon Court §2.7 (brand non-negotiables).

PR-TC-XC-053 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Form inputs are white; cards are cream; never the other way around
Steps
  1. Inspect an Input, a Card, a Section panel on the EP form.
Expected Inputs: background: #FFFFFF (panel). Cards: background: #FDFAF0 (offwhite). Section panels: background: #F4ECD3 (cream-deep). Page: background: #FBF5E5 (cream).
PR-TC-XC-054 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Required-field marker is a terracotta asterisk, not "(required)" text
Steps
  1. Open the EP form. Find a required field (e.g. Entrepreneur Name).
Expected Label ends with " *" (single terracotta asterisk). Never the words "(required)" in parentheses. Never red. Never a coloured background highlight.
PR-TC-XC-055 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Focus ring is visible on every interactive element on keyboard focus
Steps
  1. On any form, tab through every interactive element with the keyboard.
Expected Each focused element shows a 2 px terracotta ring with a 2 px cream offset. No element is invisible when focused. Mouse-clicking the same element does NOT show the ring (`:focus-visible`, not `:focus`).
PR-TC-XC-056 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Primary buttons are teal; secondary are white-on-teal-border; danger is dark-red
Steps
  1. Find primary buttons (Save, Submit), secondary (Cancel), tertiary (ghost links), danger (Delete confirmation).
Expected Primary: bg-teal text-cream. Hover → bg-sea. Secondary: bg-panel text-teal border-border. Danger: bg-danger text-cream (#9C3520).
PR-TC-XC-057 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Sidebar active item uses teal, content-area active tabs use terracotta underline
Steps
  1. Look at the sidebar — which nav item is highlighted, and what colour?
  2. Look at any tabbed page (EP detail, framework forms) — which tab is active, and how is it indicated?
Expected Sidebar active = teal background or cream-deep band (per design). Content tabs active = terracotta 2 px underline + terracotta text. These two should NOT use the same colour — the design system reserves terracotta for content-area active states (BRD/Design Memory).
PR-TC-XC-058 Negative P1 UI / UX All
No stat cards / KPI banners on tabbed forms (waste of vertical space per PM feedback)
Steps
  1. Open Networking & Mentoring tab on an EP.
  2. Open Activity Logger.
Expected No row of stat cards above filters. Filters appear directly under the page title. (Stat cards are permitted on the dedicated Dashboards only — EP Status Monitor, Sankey, Infra Monitor, Milestone Tracker, Intervention Dashboard.)
PR-TC-XC-059 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Indian number formatting (1,00,000 — not 100,000) on all monetary / count displays
Steps
  1. Find numbers ≥ 100,000 on dashboards, KPI cards, infrastructure costs, financial sums.
Expected Numbers render as 1,00,000 / 10,00,000 / 1,00,00,000 (lakhs / crores), not US-style three-digit comma grouping. Currency symbol ₹ prefix (no Rs. abbreviation). Decimal point is always a dot.
PR-TC-XC-060 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Dates display as DD-MMM-YYYY (e.g. 28-May-2026) — never US format
Steps
  1. Inspect dates in: EP card, Activity Logger row, Milestone Tracker timeline, Audit log entries.
Expected Format consistently DD-MMM-YYYY (e.g. 05-Mar-2026) in all views. NEVER 05/03/2026 (ambiguous) and NEVER 2026-03-05 in user-facing surfaces (that's developer-only). Time zones default to IST.

9. Accessibility — WCAG 2.2 AAPR-TC-XC-A11Y

Even on an internal admin tool, accessibility matters — district coordinators may have low vision or use keyboard-only.

PR-TC-XC-061 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Every interactive element is reachable by keyboard alone
Steps
  1. Mouse disabled. On the EP form, tab through every field.
  2. Tab to Save and press Enter / Space.
Expected Every input, every button, every link, every tab is reachable in a logical order. No element traps focus (cannot escape with Tab). No "ghost" focus indicators (focused but invisible).
PR-TC-XC-062 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Modal dialogs trap focus and restore it on close
Steps
  1. From EP list, click Delete on a row — confirmation dialog opens.
  2. Tab through the dialog — focus should cycle within (Cancel, Confirm).
  3. Press Escape.
Expected Focus cycles between Cancel and Confirm only. Tab does not leak to elements behind the dialog. Escape closes the dialog and returns focus to the row that opened it.
PR-TC-XC-063 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Form fields have associated labels (axe-core "label" rule passes)
Steps
  1. Run axe-core on the EP form (via Playwright).
Expected Zero violations of the label rule. Every input has either a <label for>, aria-label, or aria-labelledby.
PR-TC-XC-064 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Colour contrast meets WCAG AA
Steps
  1. Run axe-core's contrast check on EP detail, dashboard, framework form.
Expected Body text (--ink on --cream) ≥ 4.5:1; large headings ≥ 3:1; UI components ≥ 3:1. --ink-faint never used for body text. No violations.
PR-TC-XC-065 Positive P2 UI / UX All
Charts have aria-label and aria-description summarising the data
Steps
  1. Inspect dashboard charts (Sankey, donuts, bar, gauge).
Expected Each chart container has aria-label (short, e.g. "Entrepreneur status distribution") AND a <p class="sr-only"> with one or two sentences summarising the data ("Of 245 entrepreneurs, 144 are Incubated, 101 are Supported, and 0 are pending.").
PR-TC-XC-066 Positive P1 UI / UX All
prefers-reduced-motion disables non-essential transitions
Steps
  1. OS: enable Reduce Motion (macOS: Accessibility → Display; Windows: Settings → Accessibility → Visual effects).
  2. Open the app — dashboard, drawer, modal.
Expected Modal / drawer slide-in animations are disabled (instant appear). Chart entrance animations disabled. Skeleton shimmer still works at lower frequency. Functional behaviour unchanged.
PR-TC-XC-067 Positive P2 UI / UX All
Screen reader announces page route changes and form errors
Steps
  1. NVDA or VoiceOver enabled. Navigate from dashboard to EP detail.
  2. Submit a form with invalid data.
Expected Route change is announced via the AppShell's aria-live="polite" region (announces the new page title). Form errors are announced via aria-live="assertive" on the error banner.
PR-TC-XC-068 Negative P1 UI / UX All
Colour is never the only signal — every status pill / icon has accompanying text
Steps
  1. Inspect status pills: "MET", "Incubated", "Supported", "Pending", "In Progress", "Completed".
Expected Every pill has both a colour AND a text label. Never just a coloured dot/circle with no text. Never just a coloured row with no badge.

10. Performance BaselinesPR-TC-XC-PERF

Field coordinators don't have time to wait. These are the perceived-performance budgets every page must meet.

Page typeFCP targetLCP targetSave round-tripSearch/filter response
Login< 1.0 s< 1.5 s——
Dashboard (with charts)< 1.5 s< 3.0 s—< 500 ms (filter change)
List page< 1.0 s< 2.0 s—< 300 ms (filter)
Detail / Form< 1.0 s< 2.5 s< 1.5 s—
Framework form (heavy)< 1.5 s< 3.5 s< 2.0 s—
PR-TC-XC-069 Positive P0 Non-Func All
Login page meets FCP < 1 s on a 30 Mbps connection
Steps
  1. Lighthouse run on /login with Desktop preset.
Expected First Contentful Paint < 1.0 s. Largest Contentful Paint < 1.5 s. Total Blocking Time < 200 ms. Cumulative Layout Shift < 0.1.
PR-TC-XC-070 Positive P0 Non-Func SM/CTI/CTP
Dashboard page loads with all charts in < 3 s
Steps
  1. Lighthouse on /app/dashboard (or whatever the live URL is) with current data volumes (245 entrepreneurs).
Expected LCP < 3.0 s. Charts fully rendered (no skeleton remaining) at the LCP mark. Subsequent filter changes update charts in < 500 ms.
PR-TC-XC-071 Positive P1 Non-Func All
Save round-trip on EP form is < 1.5 s for a typical 50-field record
Steps
  1. Open EP edit form. Modify 5 fields. Click Save. Measure from click to "Saved" toast.
Expected ≤ 1.5 s on a healthy network. Save button shows spinner during the wait. UI is not frozen — user can still scroll the form.
PR-TC-XC-072 Positive P1 Non-Func All
List filter / search response is < 300 ms
Steps
  1. EP list. Type into the search box. Measure from last keystroke to table refresh.
Expected Debounce ~ 200 ms; backend round-trip ~ 100 ms; total perceived < 300 ms. Result count badge updates.
PR-TC-XC-073 Negative P1 Non-Func All
No memory leak when navigating between heavy pages for 30 minutes
Steps
  1. Navigate Dashboard ↔ EP list ↔ EP detail ↔ Framework form, ~ 1 navigation / 5 s, for 30 min.
  2. Watch tab memory in DevTools Performance Monitor.
Expected Tab memory grows initially then plateaus (typical SPA caching). Growth must stop. No unbounded growth past 1 GB. No browser slow-down.
PR-TC-XC-074 Negative P1 Non-Func All
No N+1 API calls on list pages
Steps
  1. Open EP list with 50 records. Inspect Network tab.
Expected One server call returns all 50 rows with their needed fields (the list endpoint fetches in batch, not per-row). No 50 separate calls.

11. Error Handling & Empty StatesPR-TC-XC-ERR

A user-friendly error story is what separates a polished app from a brittle one. Every failure mode must have a clearly defined UI.

PR-TC-XC-075 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Success toast appears for ~ 3 s after Save, then auto-dismisses
Steps
  1. Save any record. Watch the top-right of the screen.
Expected Toast: success-sft background, teal text, octicon check-circle, text "Saved." (or context-specific message). Auto-dismisses after 3 s. Hovering pauses the timer.
PR-TC-XC-076 Negative P1 UI / UX All
Inline error appears next to invalid field, AND a global "Please fix N errors" banner appears on submit
Steps
  1. On EP create form, leave Entrepreneur Name blank, fill an invalid email, and submit.
Expected Inline error under name: "Required". Inline under email: "Enter a valid email". A red banner top of form: "Please fix 2 errors and try again." Focus jumps to the first invalid field.
PR-TC-XC-077 Negative P1 UI / UX All
Server 500 errors show a friendly message, not a Python traceback
Steps
  1. Trigger a deliberate server error (e.g. send a malformed payload that bypasses client validation).
Expected Banner: "Something went wrong. Please try again. If the problem persists, contact support." No traceback, no SQL query, no Frappe internals. Backend log captures the full stack for debug.
PR-TC-XC-078 Positive P2 UI / UX All
Skeletons appear during data fetch (not generic spinners)
Steps
  1. Throttle network to Slow 3G. Open EP detail.
Expected Page chrome (sidebar, header) appears instantly. Card content shows skeleton blocks (cream-deep → offwhite shimmer). Once data arrives, skeletons swap to real content with no layout shift.
PR-TC-XC-079 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Unsaved changes warn user before navigation
Steps
  1. Open EP form. Type into Phone Number.
  2. Click the sidebar to navigate away (without saving).
Expected A dialog appears: "You have unsaved changes. Are you sure you want to leave?" with options "Stay" (default) and "Discard". Choosing Stay keeps the form intact. Discard navigates away and the field is lost.
PR-TC-XC-080 Positive P1 UI / UX All
Destructive actions (Delete, Submit final) require a typed-confirmation or explicit confirm dialog
Steps
  1. Try to delete an EP record (if your role allows).
  2. Try to set Final Selection = Incubated and save.
Expected Delete: confirmation dialog "Delete this entrepreneur record? This action cannot be undone." Confirm button is Danger variant. Final Selection: a "Are you sure? This is the official program status." dialog. Both require a deliberate click — no silent execution.

12. Locale, Number, Date & CurrencyPR-TC-XC-LOC

Indian conventions are the default. Dates are unambiguous, currency is ₹ in lakhs/crores, time is IST.

PR-TC-XC-081 Negative P1 Validation All
Date pickers reject illogical dates (e.g. 31-Feb, 32-Jan, future DOB)
Steps
  1. Open EP form, click Date Of Birth.
  2. Manually type 31-Feb-2026, 32-Jan-2026, 15-Aug-2099 (future DOB).
Expected 31-Feb and 32-Jan: rejected with "Enter a valid date." inline. Future DOB: rejected with "Date of Birth cannot be in the future." Field background gets border-error.
PR-TC-XC-082 Negative P1 Validation All
DOB < 14 years ago is rejected (minor entrepreneurs not eligible)
Steps
  1. Set DOB to 5 years ago.
Expected Inline error: "Entrepreneur must be at least 14 years old." (Adjust to actual program rule — verify with PM.)
PR-TC-XC-083 Negative P1 Validation All
Date range fields reject "end before start"
Steps
  1. Cohort start = 01-Apr-2026; cohort end = 31-Mar-2025 (in the past).
  2. Save.
Expected Save rejected; inline: "End date must be on or after the start date." Both fields highlighted.
PR-TC-XC-084 Negative P1 Validation All
Numeric fields reject letters, special chars, multiple dots
Steps
  1. On Unit Pricing → Cost field, type abc, 1.2.3, 1,000, -50.
Expected Letters and 1.2.3 are blocked at the input level. 1,000 auto-converts to 1000 (or rejects with "Use digits only"). Negative values rejected unless the field permits them; otherwise inline error.
PR-TC-XC-085 Negative P1 Validation All
Currency fields display ₹ prefix and Indian grouping
Steps
  1. Enter 1500000 into a currency field. Save and re-read.
Expected On re-read, displays as ₹ 15,00,000.00. In edit mode, the input shows the raw 1500000 without grouping (or with auto-grouping that disappears on focus, comes back on blur).
PR-TC-XC-086 Negative P1 Validation All
Phone numbers accept +91 with 10 digits, reject anything else
Steps
  1. EP phone: enter 9876543210, +919876543210, 98765 43210, 123, 98765432101 (11), abc.
Expected First three accepted (system normalises to +91 98765 43210). Last three rejected with "Enter a valid 10-digit phone number."
PR-TC-XC-087 Negative P1 Validation All
Aadhaar field accepts only 12 digits (and validates Verhoeff checksum)
Steps
  1. Enter 123456789012 (random 12 digits).
  2. Enter 234123412341 (valid Verhoeff).
  3. Enter 1234567890 (10 digits).
Expected Random 12 digits: rejected with "Invalid Aadhaar number (checksum failed)". Valid: accepted. Short: rejected. Mask should display as XXXX XXXX XXXX. Stored encrypted at rest.

Verhoeff checksum required for compliance.

PR-TC-XC-088 Negative P1 Validation All
PAN field accepts 5-letter, 4-digit, 1-letter pattern
Steps
  1. Enter ABCDE1234F.
  2. Enter abcde1234f (lowercase).
  3. Enter ABC12345DE (wrong shape).
Expected First accepted as-is. Second auto-uppercased and accepted. Third rejected with "Enter a valid PAN (e.g. ABCDE1234F)".
PR-TC-XC-089 Negative P1 Validation All
GSTIN field validates 15-character GST pattern
Steps
  1. Enter 17AAAAA0000A1Z5 (correct shape).
  2. Enter 00AAAAA0000A1Z5 (invalid state code 00).
  3. Enter random 15 alphanumeric chars.
Expected First accepted. Second and third rejected with "Enter a valid GSTIN" (state code 01–37 only; correct pattern incl. check digit).
PR-TC-XC-090 Negative P1 Validation All
Pincode field accepts only 6 digits, not starting with 0
Steps
  1. Enter 793001 (Shillong).
  2. Enter 012345.
  3. Enter 1234.
Expected First accepted. Second rejected (no Indian pincode starts with 0). Third rejected (wrong length).

13. User ManagementPR-TC-UM

Create, edit, deactivate Frappe users; assign roles; manage block restrictions; password policy; audit trail.

Who can manage users: System Manager (full) and Core Team IT (create / edit / deactivate, but cannot escalate to System Manager). Core Team Program is view-only on users. Fessociate, SELCO, Designer have no access. BRD: PR-UJ-CTI (Core Team IT journey).

13.1 Create user — happy path

PR-TC-UM-001 PositiveP0 FunctionalSM / CTI
Create a new Field Associate user with all required fields
Preconditions
  • Logged in as SM or CTI.
  • Target block "Laskein" exists in geography master.
Steps
  1. Navigate to User Management workspace → "+ New User".
  2. Fill: Email = uat-fa-test01@dhwaniris.com, First Name = UAT, Last Name = FA-Test01, Phone = +91 9876543210.
  3. Set Roles: check "Field Associate" only.
  4. Set Block restriction = "Laskein" (block-bound).
  5. Set Send welcome email = Yes.
  6. Click Save.
Expected Toast: "User created successfully." User row appears in list with status "Active" and "Welcome email sent". Email arrives at the address within 2 min containing a one-time password-set link. Audit log records the creation with timestamp + creator.

BRD: PR-UJ-CTI §User Management.

PR-TC-UM-002 PositiveP0 FunctionalSM / CTI
New user can set password via welcome email link and log in
Preconditions
  • UM-001 ran; welcome email received.
Steps
  1. Click the link in the welcome email.
  2. Set a strong password meeting policy (≥ 10 chars, mix of upper / lower / digit / symbol).
  3. Submit.
  4. At the login page, sign in with the new credentials.
Expected Password set succeeds. Login lands on the FA landing (Entrepreneurs list, scoped to Laskein). User's avatar/name visible top-left. Block restriction visible (sidebar shows "Block: Laskein").
PR-TC-UM-003 PositiveP1 FunctionalSM / CTI
Create users for each of the 6 roles using the API (bulk seed for UAT)
Steps
  1. Use admin API token 2b7ed3e7f3863d3:b65a809444a7792.
  2. POST /api/method/frappe.client.insert with payload {doctype:"User", email:"uat-sm@dhwaniris.com", first_name:"UAT", last_name:"SM", roles:[{role:"System Manager"}]}.
  3. Repeat for: uat-cti (Core Team IT), uat-ctp (Core Team Program), uat-fa (Field Associate), uat-selco (SELCO Executive), uat-designer (Designer).
Expected Each call returns 200 with the new user JSON. Listing users in UI shows all 6 with correct roles. Each can log in (after password reset link).

Setup step for the rest of UAT. Documented separately in §3.

BRD: PR-UJ-FA — Fessociates are block-bound.

PR-TC-UM-007 NegativeP1 ValidationSM / CTI

OWASP A01 Broken Access Control.

Email must be lowercase and trimmed before save

  1. Enter email Test@Dhwaniris.COM (leading/trailing spaces, mixed case).

13.3 Edit, deactivate, delete

PR-TC-UM-010 PositiveP0 FunctionalSM / CTI
Edit user phone, name, block — changes persist
Steps
  1. Open user uat-fa-test01.
  2. Change First Name to "UAT-Updated".
  3. Change Block from Laskein to Khliehriat.
  4. Save.
  5. Log out / log in as that user.
Expected Save toast. List view reflects new name. After re-login, the user now sees entrepreneurs from Khliehriat block; Laskein records are no longer visible.
PR-TC-UM-011 PositiveP0 FunctionalSM / CTI
Deactivate a user — they cannot log in until reactivated
Steps
  1. Open uat-fa-test01. Set Enabled = No. Save.
  2. Sign out, attempt to log in as uat-fa-test01.
Expected Login rejected with "Your account has been disabled. Please contact your administrator." No session cookie issued. Audit log records the deactivation.
PR-TC-UM-012 PositiveP1 FunctionalSM / CTI
Active sessions for a deactivated user are revoked within 60 s
Steps
  1. uat-fa-test01 is logged in on Browser A.
  2. SM disables them via Browser B.
  3. Within 60 s, uat-fa-test01 (still in Browser A) clicks any action.
Expected Any next API call returns 401 / 403; user is forcibly redirected to login. (Frappe's session check verifies enabled on each request.)
PR-TC-UM-013 NegativeP1 FunctionalSM / CTI
Cannot deactivate the only System Manager account (system would lock itself)
Steps
  1. If only one SM exists, try to disable it.
Expected Save rejected with "Cannot disable the last System Manager account. Create another System Manager first." User remains enabled.
PR-TC-UM-014 NegativeP1 FunctionalSM
Cannot delete a user who owns records — soft-delete / archive instead
Steps
  1. Try to permanently delete uat-fa-test01 (who has created 2 EP records).
Expected Delete rejected with "This user is the owner of 2 Entrepreneur records. Reassign or disable instead." The UI offers an "Archive" alternative that keeps history.

13.4 Password policy

PR-TC-UM-015 PositiveP1 ValidationAll
Password set page enforces minimum strength rules
Steps
  1. On password set page, try: abc, password, Password1, P@ssw0rd!2026.
Expected Strength meter visible. abc = weak/rejected. password = rejected (common dictionary word). Password1 = weak (rejected if min length is 10). P@ssw0rd!2026 = strong, accepted.

Recommend zxcvbn or similar; verify policy in Frappe System Settings.

PR-TC-UM-016 NegativeP1 ValidationAll
Cannot reuse last 5 passwords on reset
Steps
  1. Change password 5 times. On the 6th change, try to set it back to the original.
Expected Rejected with "You cannot reuse a recent password. Please choose a new one." (Adjust to actual policy; recommend ≥ 5.)
PR-TC-UM-017 NegativeP1 ValidationAll
Password cannot equal email, name, or contain the username
Steps
  1. For user uat-fa-test01, try to set password to uat-fa-test01 or FA-Test01.
Expected Rejected with: "Password cannot contain your username or name."

13.5 Role-permission deep dive

PR-TC-UM-018 NegativeP0 SecurityFA
Field Associate cannot access User Management workspace
Steps
  1. Logged in as FA, manually visit /app/user.
Expected 403 Forbidden page or redirect to FA landing. Sidebar does not show User Management item.
PR-TC-UM-019 NegativeP0 SecurityCTP
Core Team Program has view-only on User list (no Create/Edit buttons)
Steps
  1. Logged in as CTP, open User Management.
Expected List visible. "+ New User" button absent. Clicking any user row opens read-only view (no Edit button, all fields disabled).
PR-TC-UM-020 NegativeP0 SecurityFA
Fessociate cannot see entrepreneurs from another block via API
Steps
  1. Logged in as uat-fa (assigned to Block A).
  2. Call GET /api/method/frappe.client.get_list?doctype=Enterprenur Profile&filters=[["block","=","Block B"]].
Expected API returns empty list (not 403) — Frappe applies user permission filters automatically. Even if the user crafts a filter for Block B, the backend strips it down to their permitted blocks. Network response contains no record from Block B.
PR-TC-UM-021 NegativeP0 SecurityFA
Fessociate cannot fetch a specific entrepreneur from another block via direct URL
Steps
  1. Get the name of an EP in Block B (via SM session).
  2. As uat-fa (Block A), call GET /api/resource/Enterprenur Profile/<EP-name>.
Expected 403 Forbidden with "You do not have permission to access this document."

14. Masters & Reference DataPR-TC-MS

All lookup tables underpinning the application: Sector, Geography (District / Block / Village), Cohort, Business Basket, Framework Task Master, Document Type, Mentor Master, Material Master, Packaging Master, Sector Master, etc.

Who manages masters: System Manager & Core Team IT only. Core Team Program view-only. Field-level roles cannot see Masters at all. Bulk imports allowed for geography, sectors, business baskets, and the 351-row Framework Task Master seed.

14.1 Sector master

PR-TC-MS-001 PositiveP0 FunctionalSM / CTI
Create a new Sector "[UAT] Apiculture" with Business Baskets linked
Steps
  1. Masters → Sector → +New.
  2. Sector Name = "[UAT] Apiculture". Description = "Honey and bee products".
  3. Add 2 Business Baskets: "Raw honey", "Beeswax candles" in the child table.
  4. Save.
Expected Sector saved. Now appears in EP form's Sector dropdown. Selecting it cascades Business Basket dropdown to show the 2 baskets only.
PR-TC-MS-002 NegativeP1 ValidationSM / CTI
Duplicate sector name rejected (case-insensitive)
Steps
  1. Try to create "[UAT] APICULTURE" or "[uat] apiculture".
Expected Rejected with "A sector with this name already exists." Comparison is case-insensitive and trims whitespace.
PR-TC-MS-003 NegativeP1 ValidationSM / CTI
Cannot delete a sector that is in use by any EP record
Steps
  1. Link an EP to "[UAT] Apiculture".
  2. Try to delete the sector.
Expected Delete rejected: "This sector is in use by 1 entrepreneur. Reassign or archive instead." Offer an "Archive" option (sets a deactivated flag — sector no longer appears in new dropdowns but historical records still resolve correctly).

15. Entrepreneur Profile — Full LifecyclePR-TC-EP

The most heavily-used record in the system. Covers onboarding, profiling, rating, selection, prioritisation, networking, log book, and lifecycle transitions (MET → Incubated / Supported).

Lifecycle order: Selection → Status by CTIT → Prioritisation → Diagnostics. Frameworks come AFTER selection, not before.
Status values: MET (any saved profile), Incubated, Supported. No Rejected / Pending.
Who can set final status: CTIT (Core Team Program) only. Field Associates fill the 10Q + Rural E-Champ during profiling. (BRD: Decisions table.)

15.1 EP onboarding — happy path (web CRM)

PR-TC-EP-001 PositiveP0 FunctionalFA / SM / CTP
Create a new EP with all required fields filled
Preconditions
  • Logged in as FA on Block "Laitkroh".
  • Test photo + Aadhaar / PAN images present in tests/fixtures/files/.
  • Cohort "[UAT] Cohort 2026-29" active.
Steps
  1. EP list → +New Entrepreneur.
  2. About Entrepreneur: Name = "[UAT] Honey Farmer One", DOB = 15-Apr-1985, Gender = Female, Education = 10th, Marital = Married, Family Size = 5-10, Language = Khasi.
  3. Status & Cohort: Activity Status = Active, Cohort = "[UAT] Cohort 2026-29", Visit Date = today, Intervention Date = today.
  4. About Enterprise: Enterprise Name = "Hilltop Honey", Business Start Date = 01-Jan-2020, Position = Founder, Enterprise Stage = Startup, Sector = Apiculture, Business Basket = "Raw honey", Market Accessibility = Local.
  5. Contact: Phone = +91 9876543210, Email = honeyfarm@example.com.
  6. Location: District = East Khasi Hills, Block = Laitkroh, Village = Mawphlang (or first in list), GPS captured (or manual lat/lon).
  7. Documents: Upload Profile Photo, Aadhaar (12-digit valid), PAN (valid pattern).
  8. Click Save.
Expected Saved. EP-name like EP-[UAT] Honey Farmer One-00001 auto-generated. Toast: "Saved." Profile Dashboard tab loads with hero card, basic info, and an empty Diagnostic Framework block (no priorities set yet). Activity Status = "MET". Final Selection = blank (will be set by CTIT later).

BRD: PR-EP-001.

PR-TC-EP-002 PositiveP1 FunctionalFA
Profile picture upload preview shows immediately, file persists after save
Steps
  1. Click profile picture upload, pick a 500 KB JPEG.
  2. Verify preview appears.
  3. Save the form. Re-open.
Expected Preview renders before save (data URL). After save, image URL points to Frappe's File doctype path. Re-open shows the same image, sized to fit. Image is private (not accessible without auth).
PR-TC-EP-003 PositiveP1 FunctionalFA
GPS capture: click "Use my location" populates lat/lng + reverse-geocodes to village
Steps
  1. On EP form, Location section, click "Use my location" (or whatever the GPS button is labelled).
  2. Allow browser geolocation prompt.
Expected Lat / lng populated (6+ decimal places). Map marker appears. If the user is within a known village polygon, Village dropdown auto-suggests. Manual override still possible.
PR-TC-EP-004 NegativeP1 FunctionalFA
GPS denied gracefully — manual lat/lng still works

16. Product ProfilePR-TC-PR

Products belong to entrepreneurs. Each product has details, process flow, variants (SKUs), and financials. Source-of-truth = client mockup product_profile_module.html.

  2. Drawer opens. Fill: Product Name (from Product Master), Sector, Product Snapshot, tick Available Months (Jan/Feb/Mar), Shelf Life Duration = "12 months".
  3. Save.
Expected Product card appears in the strip with name + category badge. Counter "Products: N" updates on the EP card.

  2. Pick a Product Name from the Product Master autocomplete; save.
Expected Without a name: "Product name is required." Product Name is a Link to the Product Master (autocomplete), not free text. [A duplicate-per-EP block is NOT a confirmed rule in the wireframe — confirm with BA before testing it.]
PR-TC-PR-003 NegativeP1 ValidationFA / CTP
Shelf Life Duration is a free-text field (e.g. "12 months")
Steps
  1. Enter Shelf Life Duration = "12 months".
Expected Accepted — Shelf Life Duration is a free-text Data field; the wireframe has no numeric/positive-integer validation. [If a numeric months value with validation is required, that is a spec change — confirm with BA.]
PR-TC-PR-004 PositiveP1 UI / UXFA / CTP
Available Months is a 12-row checkbox table (drives the Monthly Production Tracker)

  1. Open the form. Available Months section. Tick Jan and Jun.
Expected Available Months is a 12-row checkbox table (TRUE/FALSE per month) — not a chip group. The ticked months become the rows of the Monthly Production Tracker; at least one month must be ticked to generate the tracker.

BRD: Available Months drive the Monthly Production Tracker (checkbox-table model, per wireframe).

17. The 27 Diagnostic FrameworksPR-TC-FW

All frameworks share a common structural pattern (tabs, required fields, child tables, log book, intervention details). The Common Framework Tests (17.0) apply to every framework. The per-framework subsections (17.1 – 17.27) capture only the unique behaviour for each.

Run pattern: Pick a candidate framework, run all common tests, then run the framework-specific tests. Repeat across 5 representative frameworks for full UAT confidence; the remaining 22 can be smoke-tested via the common suite only.

17.0 Common Framework Tests (run for each of the 27)

PR-TC-FW-COM-001 PositiveP0 FunctionalFA / CTP
Framework page loads from EP's diagnostics navigation
Steps
  1. Open EP → Diagnostics tab. Click any framework with priority set.
Expected Framework form loads in < 2 s. Header shows EP name + framework name. All defined tabs render. No JS console errors.
PR-TC-FW-COM-002 PositiveP1 UI / UXFA / CTP
All tabs render: per-framework tabs + Log Book + Intervention Details + Resources
Steps
  1. Click each tab.
Expected Each tab activates with terracotta underline. Content loads (skeleton then real). No tab silently fails or shows blank.

BRD Rule 6: Intervention Details on every framework.
BRD Rule 8: Log Book per-framework, only this framework's activities.

PR-TC-FW-COM-003 PositiveP0 FunctionalFA / CTP
Save with valid data succeeds; progress on EP profile dashboard updates
Steps
  1. Fill required fields in the first tab.
  2. Save.
  3. Return to EP profile dashboard.
Expected Toast "Saved.". Progress bar for this framework on EP dashboard moves up.
PR-TC-FW-COM-004 NegativeP0 ValidationFA / CTP
Required fields enforce save validation
Steps
  1. Empty form. Save.
Expected Inline errors on all required fields; top banner counts errors; focus first invalid.
PR-TC-FW-COM-005 PositiveP1 FunctionalFA
Log Book tab shows ONLY this framework's activities (Rule 8)
Steps
  1. Log 1 activity on this framework via Activity Logger, 1 on another framework.
  2. Open Log Book tab here.
Expected Only the activity logged against THIS framework appears. The other framework's activity does not pollute.
PR-TC-FW-COM-006 PositiveP1 FunctionalFA / CTP
Intervention Details tab captures narrative + supporting docs (Rule 6)
Steps
  1. Intervention Details tab → write a short narrative + attach a PDF.
  2. Save.
Expected Persisted. Independent of Required tab. Visible to all roles with read access.
PR-TC-FW-COM-007 NegativeP0 SecuritySELCO / Designer
Role-restricted frameworks block other roles
Steps
  1. SELCO opens a non-Infra framework — should fail.
  2. Designer opens a non-Branding framework — should fail.
Expected 403 / route deny.
PR-TC-FW-COM-008 NegativeP1 FunctionalFA / CTP
Concurrent edit guard fires
Steps
  1. Two users edit the same framework record on the same EP simultaneously.
  2. Both save.
Expected Second saver gets "This document was modified after you loaded it."
PR-TC-FW-COM-009 PositiveP1 UI / UXFA / CTP
All child tables use 6-column standard layout: # / Field / Type / Mandatory / Notes / Action
Steps
  1. Inspect any framework's child table.
Expected 6-col header per BRD pattern. Add Row / Delete Row buttons visible. Edit inline.
PR-TC-FW-COM-010 PositiveP1 FunctionalFA / CTP
Auto-save (or save-on-blur) preserves typing on field change
Steps
  1. Type into a text field. Tab out without clicking Save.
  2. Refresh page.
Expected If auto-save: value persisted, refresh restores. If not auto-save: warning dialog before refresh ("unsaved changes"). Either is fine — but the behaviour must be consistent across all frameworks.
PR-TC-FW-COM-011 PositiveP1 APIAll
REST GET / POST on framework doctype works with auth
Steps
  1. GET /api/resource/<DF Doctype>/<name> with API token.
  2. POST update.
Expected Standard Frappe REST behaviour. 200 / 201 / 4xx with clear errors.
PR-TC-FW-COM-012 NegativeP1 Non-FuncFA / CTP
Heavy framework form (50+ fields, multiple child tables) loads in < 3 s
Steps
  1. Open the Infrastructure framework (one of the heaviest).
Expected Page interactive in < 3 s on 30 Mbps. Skeletons during load. Tabs lazy-load their content.

17.20 Logistic Service

Route-based: Assessment + leg tables + frequency → monthly/annual cost.

PR-TC-FW-LSVC-001 PositiveP1 FunctionalFA / CTP
Add a route with legs + a frequency; monthly/annual cost auto-computed (route-frequency model)
Steps
  1. Existing tab → + Add Logistics Route. Set Route name, Direction = Outbound, Frequency = Weekly (the build's frequency multipliers: Daily ×30/month · Twice a week · Weekly ×4 · Twice a month ×2 · Monthly ×1 · Every 2 months ×0.5).
  2. Save once (legs need the saved parent route ID), then + Add Leg ×2: Leg 1 Mawphlang → Shillong, Cost ₹ 500; Leg 2 Shillong → Guwahati, Cost ₹ 1,500.
Expected Frequency sets Trips/Month at the route level (not per leg). Total Cost Per Trip = Σ leg costs = 500 + 1,500 = ₹ 2,000. Trips/Month = 4 (Weekly). Monthly Cost = Total Cost Per Trip × Trips/Month = 2,000 × 4 = ₹ 8,000. Annual Cost = Monthly × 12 = ₹ 96,000. The All-Routes total bar sums Monthly/Annual across routes. [Verified live, S26 14-Jun-2026: ₹2,000 / 4 / ₹8,000 / ₹96,000.]

  1. Client-side responsibility per RFP. Schedule the agency's VAPT 4 weeks before go-live.
Expected VAPT report shows no Critical or High findings. Medium findings remediated or risk-accepted with sign-off.

Solution Doc Assumption: VAPT is client responsibility.

24. Session-23 BRD Reconciliation — Permissions, Status Model & KPIsPR-TC-S23

Cases added/updated on 10-Jun-2026 to align the master with the BRD (PR-OV-004 permission matrix) and the Session-23 PM design rulings (Q-A…Q-F) + the EP status-model redesign + the Landscape KPI redesign. Each card cites its BRD source and the existing case it supersedes. Items marked UPDATES change the Expected result of an existing case; NEW covers behaviour not previously tested.

24.1 Role permission enforcement (deny + positive paths)

Specialist/Program roles must be scoped server-side, not just in the nav. Exercises the deny paths behind Bugs 73/75/76.

PR-TC-SEC-030NegativeP0SecurityDesigner
Designer cannot CREATE a framework record (no create permission)
Preconditions
  • Logged in as Designer.
Steps
  1. Open Diagnostics → Branding Identity → click "+ New" (or POST frappe.client.insert for DF Branding Identity).
  2. Repeat the API insert for a non-Marketing framework (e.g. DF Financials).
Expected No create path exists: the "+ New" action is absent/disabled, and a direct API insert is rejected 403 server-side for every framework. Designer edits existing records only.

Source: BRD PR-OV-004 — Designer = "View + Edit own drafts … no Create no Delete". NEW (gap exposed by Bug 73).

PR-TC-SEC-031NegativeP0SecurityDesigner
Designer cannot reach non-Marketing workspaces via direct URL or API
Preconditions
  • Logged in as Designer.
Steps
  1. Direct-navigate to /primerural/ (Landscape), /entrepreneurs, /products, /masters, and /d/DF Financials.
  2. Call get_list on Enterprenur Profile, Sector, Cohort, and non-Marketing DF * doctypes.
Expected Every one is denied — UI shows the permission-denied page; API returns 403 / empty. Designer has no read or write outside Branding/Label/Brochure. (Today: Landscape + all frameworks + 49-doctype Masters are reachable and EP data is readable.)

Source: BRD PR-OV-004 — all non-Marketing cells = "--" (server-enforced). NEW (Bug 73: confidentiality leak — reads all EP/Progress Report).

PR-TC-SEC-032NegativeP1SecuritySELCO
SELCO cannot edit non-SELCO (Built-Environment) fields, cannot create, cannot leave Infrastructure
Preconditions
  • Logged in as SELCO Executive; an Infrastructure record exists.
Steps
  1. Open the Infrastructure record → Built-Environment tab → attempt to edit a civil field (e.g. Plinth Rate / SQM, Land/Rent fields).
  2. Attempt to create a new Infrastructure record (+ New) and to open any non-Infrastructure framework / EP / Masters.
Expected BE (civil) fields are read-only — edit is blocked and Save does not enable; SELCO edits only EE/CE + SELCO pricing/equipment/disbursement fields. No "+ New" (no create). All non-Infrastructure workspaces denied. (Today: editing Plinth Rate enabled Save = Bug 75.)

Source: BRD PR-OV-004 — SELCO = "View all tabs (BE/EE/CE); edit only SELCO-relevant fields … no Create no Delete". UPDATES the SELCO row-scope assumption; NEW deny detail (Bug 75).

PR-TC-SEC-034NegativeP0SecurityCT-Program
CT-Program is view-only on Users and Masters (no create / edit / delete)
Preconditions
  • Logged in as Core Team Program.
Steps
  1. Open User Manager and a Master (Sector / Cohort).
  2. Attempt create, edit, and delete on each — via UI and via frappe.client.insert/set_value/delete.
Expected Read works; create / edit / delete are all blocked (UI controls absent, API 403). has_permission for User/Sector/Cohort create+write+delete = false. (Today: all return true = Bug 76 — CT-Program can delete users + wipe masters.)

Source: BRD PR-OV-004 — CT-Program = "view-only" Users + Masters. UPDATES PR-TC-UM/PR-TC-MS role rows; NEW deny detail (Bug 76).

PR-TC-SEC-036PositiveP1SecurityDesigner/SELCO
Specialist positive path — edit own framework's existing record
Preconditions
  • A Branding (for Designer) / Infrastructure (for SELCO) record already created by the FA.
Steps
  1. Designer: open the Branding record, upload/edit a draft (Label/Brand/Brochure) field, Save.
  2. SELCO: open the Infrastructure record, edit a SELCO field (pricing / equipment status / disbursement), Save.
Expected Edit + Save succeed on the assigned framework's existing record (this is the role's one allowed action). Confirms scoping removes everything else but preserves the legitimate edit.

Source: BRD PR-OV-004. NEW positive control.

24.2 EP status model + Final Selection

Status is two orthogonal fields; MET/Active redefined; Final Selection attachment mandatory.

PR-TC-EP-050PositiveP0FunctionalCTIT/CTP
EP status = two orthogonal fields: selection_status + engagement_status
Steps
  1. On an EP, set selection_status = Incubated and engagement_status = Discontinued.
  2. Reload; check the Landscape funnel + Active count.
Expected Both persist independently — an EP can be Incubated and Discontinued (selection outcome retained, engagement ended). selection_status ∈ {MET→Incubated|Supported}; engagement_status ∈ {Active, Discontinued}. (Replaces the single mutually-exclusive enum {Active,Incubated,Supported}.)

Source: S23 PM decision (two-field model). NEW — supersedes any single-status case in §15.

PR-TC-EP-051NegativeP1FunctionalCTIT/CTP
Final Selection requires a supporting attachment (mandatory gate)
Steps
  1. Set Final Selection = Incubated (or Supported) with no attachment uploaded.
  2. Save.
Expected Save is blocked with a clear "attachment required" message until a supporting document is attached. (Today the gate is not enforced — Bug 50.)

Source: BRD PR-TC-EP-021 + S23 PM ruling Q-F (mandatory). UPDATES PR-TC-EP-021.

24.3 Landscape KPI cards

MET replaces Total; Active redefined; Blocks Covered added; coverage cards use distinct non-null geo.

PR-TC-DB-060PositiveP1FunctionalCTIT/CTP/DC
Landscape KPI card set + definitions
Steps
  1. Open Landscape; read the KPI cards.
Expected Cards = MET (= count of all saved EPs) · Active (= engagement_status ≠ Discontinued, includes Incubated/Supported) · Incubated · Supported · GPS Verified · Districts Covered · Blocks Covered · Village Visits. There is no "Total Entrepreneurs" card (MET is the headline total). MET must equal the EP-list count. (Today: Total=18 + MET card=Active card=15 duplicate — Bugs 64/68.)

Source: S23 PM KPI redesign + Q-D. NEW — supersedes Landscape KPI cases in §19 referencing "Total Entrepreneurs"/MET-as-profiled-only.

PR-TC-DB-061PositiveP2FunctionalCTIT/CTP/DC
Districts/Blocks Covered = distinct non-null geo; Village-Visits mode hides EP widgets
Steps
  1. Read Districts Covered + Blocks Covered.
  2. Switch map mode to "Village Visits".
Expected Districts Covered = COUNT(DISTINCT district WHERE district != ''); Blocks Covered = same over block. In Village-Visits mode the entrepreneur widgets (BY SECTOR panel + MET/Active/Incubated/Supported/GPS cards) are hidden; only visit-relevant widgets show. (Today: BY SECTOR + entrepreneur cards persist — Bugs 71/62.)

Source: S23 PM KPI redesign (Bug 69) + Q-on mode-context (Bugs 71/62). NEW.

24.4 Design rulings (Q-A, Q-B, Q-C, Q-E)

PR-TC-AL-040PositiveP1FunctionalFA
Activity Logger default scope + widenable Field-Associate filter (Q-A)
Steps
  1. Open Activity Logger as an FA.
  2. Change the Field-Associate filter to another fellow in the same district.
  3. Try to widen beyond own district.
Expected On load a default filter = own district + own block + self (so the default view is own logs). The Field-Associate filter works and can be widened up to own district / all blocks (other fellows' logs become visible). Widening beyond own district is not allowed. (Today: hard self-scope + the field_associate filter is ignored — Bugs 60/67.)

Source: S23 PM ruling Q-A. UPDATES PR-TC-AL scope cases.

PR-TC-VS-020NegativeP2FunctionalFA/CTP
Village Survey is one-per-village (2nd survey to same village is rejected — by design)
Steps
  1. Create a Village Survey for village X; save.
  2. Attempt a second survey for the same village X.
Expected The second attempt is rejected (duplicate village_id / 409) — this is intended, not a bug. One survey record per village, re-edited over time. (Resolves the Session-20 "repeat-visit?" design flag.)

Source: S23 PM ruling Q-C (autoname=village_id intended).

PR-TC-PR-030PositiveP2FunctionalFA/CTP
Product Sector auto-derives from Business Basket and is read-only (Q-E)
Steps
  1. On a Product, pick a Business Basket (e.g. Candy).
  2. Observe Sector; attempt to set a different Sector manually.
Expected Sector auto-fills from the Basket (Candy → Food Processing) and is read-only — a manual Sector pick is not possible / does not override. (Today it auto-derives but silently overrides a manual pick instead of being read-only — confusing; cf. Bug 49 family.)

Source: S23 PM ruling Q-E (auto-derive wins; make field read-only).

PR-TC-NT-030PositiveP3FunctionalAll
Bell mark-read syncs the Notification Center record's read_at (Q-B)
Steps
  1. Receive a Notification Center notification (unread).
  2. Click the bell row to mark it read.
  3. Open Notification Center; check the record's Read/read_at.
Expected Marking read via the bell also sets the Notification Center record's read_at — read state is consistent across both views. (Today the two stores don't cross-sync — Bug 61 minor.)

Source: S23 PM ruling Q-B.
